)@@G@@TIPB        @@@@@@)K[@@@. ADDRESS WHICH POINTS TO THE ACTUAL MFD ITEM INFT
)@@G@@TO A RELATIVE     @F@@@@. ADDRESS THAT POINTS TO THE COPY OF THAT ITEM IFU
)@@G@@N THE DGET$ FILE. @B@@@@. IT MAKES USE OF TWO FACTS TO DO THIS:   @[@@@@FV
)@@G@@.     @E@@@@.    1. THE MFD IS COPIED TO THE DGET$ FILE TRACK BY TRACK. FW
)@@G@@@F@@@@.       THEREFORE, IF A GIVEN ITEM STARTS AT SECTOR 49 OR WORD    FX
)@@G@@@G@@@@.       1372 WITHIN SOME GIVEN TRACK OF THE MFD, THEN IT WILL STARFY
)@@G@@T     @F@@@@.       AT SECTOR 49 OR WORD 1372 OF THE COPY OF THAT TRACK FZ
)@@G@@IN    @G@@@@.       OUR DGET$ FILE.  ALL WE NEED TO DO IS FIND THE RIGHTGA
)@@G@@ TRACK.     @G@@@@.    2. THE DGET$ FILE CONTAINS COPIES OF EACH DIRECTOGB
)@@G@@RY ALLOCATION     @G@@@@.       SECTOR (DAS).  THE DAS CONTAINS THE ADDRGC
)@@G@@ESS OF THE MFD TRACK    @G@@@@.       FROM WHICH IT WAS COPIED, AS WELL GD
)@@G@@AS THE MFD ADDRESSES FROM     @E@@@@.       WHICH THE NEXT FEW (UP TO 8)GE
)@@G@@ TRACKS WERE COPIED.    @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. DURING THE FOLLOWING ROUTINEGF
)@@G@@, WE READ EVERY DAS IN THE DGET$ FILE.    @G@@@@. FROM EACH ONE WE PULL GG
)@@G@@OUT THE MFD ADDRESS OF EACH TRACK DESCRIBED IN  @G@@@@. THE DAS.  THESE GH
)@@G@@ARE BUILT INTO A TABLE CALLED ADDTBL.  POSITION IN    @F@@@@. ADDTBL INDGI
)@@G@@ICATES POSITION IN THE DGET$ FILE (EG, THE 7TH WORD OF@F@@@@. ADDTBL CONGJ
)@@G@@TAINS THE MFD ADDRESS FROM WHICH MSCON$ COPIED THE 7TH@G@@@@. TRACK OF DGK
)@@G@@IRECTORY ITEMS INTO THE DGET$ FILE).  NOTE THAT THIS IS     @G@@@@. ALL GL
)@@G@@ZERO-RELATIVE.  ALSO NOTE THAT TRACK ZERO OF THE DGET$ FILE IS    @F@@@@GM
)@@G@@. NOT TRACK ZERO OF DIRECTORY ITEMS:  THE BEGINNING OF THE DGET$  @F@@@@GN
)@@G@@. FILE CONSISTS OF A TABLE OF CONTENTS AND THE LOOKUP TABLE.  THE @F@@@@GO
)@@G@@. TRACK NUMBER OF THE FIRST TRACK IN THE DGET$ FILE WHICH CONTAINS@F@@@@GP
)@@G@@. DIRECTORY ITEMS IS RETURNED BY MSCON$, IN WORD 2,,H1 OF SECTOR 0@F@@@@GQ
)@@G@@. OF THE FILE.  THIS IS THE TRACK WHICH WAS COPIED FROM THE MFD   @C@@@@GR
)@@G@@. LOCATION WHOSE ADDRESS IS IN WORD 0 OF ADDTBL.@[@@@@.     @F@@@@. AFTEGS
)@@G@@R INITIALIZATION IS COMPLETE, CALLS MAY BE MADE TO DIRLNK TO@E@@@@. READGT
)@@G@@ A SECTOR CORRESPONDING TO A GIVEN MFD (LINK) ADDRESS.@G@@@@. FIRST WE SGU
)@@G@@EARCH ADDTBL TO FIND THE ADDRESS OF A TRACK WHICH WOULD     @F@@@@. CONTGV
)@@G@@AIN THE ADDRESS WE ARE LOOKING FOR.  THE INDEX INTO ADDTBL  @F@@@@. IS TGW
)@@G@@HE RELATIVE TRACK NUMBER IN THE DGET$ FILE FOR THE FIND.    @F@@@@. THE GX
)@@G@@OFFSET INTO THE TRACK IS DETERMINED FROM THE DIFFERENCE     @G@@@@. BETWGY
)@@G@@EEN THE ADDRESS WE ARE LOOKING FOR AND THE MFD ADDRESS OF THE     @F@@@@GZ
)@@G@@. TRACK IT IS IN (FROM ADDTBL).  THIS OFFSET INTO THE TRACK IN THE@A@@@@HA
)@@G@@. DGET$ FILE GIVES THE ITEM WE WANT.@[@@@@.     @D@@@@.                 HB
)@@G@@                    DWIGHT ARTHUR   @D@@@@.                             HC
)@@G@@        BOSTON, MAY 1976@[@@@@.     @E@@@@          L         A0,QSEC   HD
)@@G@@        # OF DIRECTORY SECTORS@G@@@@          AN        A0,NXSEC        HE
)@@G@@  SUBTRACT ADDR OF FIRST SECTOR     @G@@@@          SSL       A0,6      HF
)@@G@@        CONVERT SECTOR COUNT TO TRACKS    @E@@@@          TG,U      A0,AHG
)@@G@@DDSIZ+1       IS ADDTBL BIG ENOUGH? @G@@@@          J         OVFL      HH
)@@G@@        NO, RETURN ERROR STATUS TO USER   @ @@@@          ON        PRE3HI
)@@G@@3     @E@@@@          TZ        DIR$MFDF          NEW (MFDF) FORMAT?    HJ
)@@G@@@F@@@@          J         NOMCT             YES, ALL SECTOR ADDRESSES   HK
)@@G@@@E@@@@.                                        (DON'T NEED MCT)   @G@@@@HL
)@@G@@          L,U       A0,MCTPKT         GET MASTER CONFIGURATION TABLE    HM
)@@G@@@^@@@@          ER        MCT$@D@@@@          TZ,S1     MCTPKT          HN

)@@G@@    . @ @@@@          OFF       PRE33     @F@@@@          L         A0,NHU
)@@G@@XSEC          GET ADDR OF FIRST DIR SECTOR@F@@@@          S         A0,IHV
)@@G@@OPAK+5        SET FOR READ OF FIRST DAS   @F@@@@.                       HW

)@@G@@1,0)          SET INDEX INTO ADDTBL @E@@@@          LXI,U     A2,3      HY

)@@G@@@G@@@@/. DIRLED - GIVEN A LEAD ITEM LINK ADDRESS (AS FROM THE LOOKUP TABRY
)@@G@@LE,   @G@@@@.           A SEARCH ITEM, OR A MAIN ITEM BACK LINK), FIND TRZ
)@@G@@HE SECTOR   @G@@@@.           IT POINTS TO, AND PLACE IT IN LBUF FOR DIRSA
)@@G@@SEC.  IF THE USER @H@@@@.           WANTS LEAD ITEMS (AS INDICATED IN THSB
)@@G@@E DIRINT MASK), THEN GIVE     @G@@@@.           IT TO HIM, ALSO.  ON SUBSC
)@@G@@SEQUENT CALLS, IF THE LEAD ITEM IS  @G@@@@.           STILL IN CORE (GOTSD
)@@G@@ONE IS NONZERO), JUST MERGE INTO DIRSEC   @E@@@@.           CODE AND RETSE
)@@G@@URN THE MAIN ITEMS TO THE USER.     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@.      FORTRAN:  CSF

)@@G@@S TO USER   @F@@@@/. DIRLUT - RETURNS LUT SECTORS ONE AT A TIME TO USER'YA

)@@G@@ALL DIRLUF (ECODE,$ERR,QUALFL,LUTW) @[@@@@.     @A@@@@.      ASSEMBLY: LBC

)@@G@@           <ERROR RETURN>       A1,A2 CONTAINS ERROR CODE   @A@@@@.     BE

)@@G@@ADDRESS OF A 4-WORD BUFFER CONTAINING THE @A@@@@. FIELDATA QUALIFIER ANDBG
)@@G@@ FILENAME.  @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. FOR FORTRAN CALLS, THE RESULTING LEAD ITBH

)@@G@@TURNED IN A0.     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. IF AN ERROR IS ENCOUNTERED IN THE BJ
)@@G@@SEARCH ITEM CHAIN, THE ERROR RETURN @D@@@@. WILL BE TAKEN, WITH ECODE (ABK
)@@G@@1) SET TO 'LUFERR'.     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@LUFARG    EQU       4         BL

)@@G@@@A@@@@          DO DEBUG>0 , SLJ TON$     @F@@@@          TZ        ADDLBU

)@@G@@/. GETLUT - SUBROUTINE TO GET THE DESIRED LUT SECTOR. @[@@@@.     @F@@@@DU
)@@G@@. ENTER WITH DGET$ FILE SECTOR # IN A0.  READS UP THE SECTOR, IF  @F@@@@DV
)@@G@@. NECESSARY, AND SETS A0 TO THE ADDRESS OF THE SECTOR IN CORE.    @[@@@@DW
)@@G@@.     @ @@@@. DESTROYS X11, A0, A2, A3    @[@@@@.     @F@@@@GETLUT    LADX
)@@G@@        A2,LUTRD+5        GET FIRST SECTOR IN CORE    @D@@@@          TLDY
)@@G@@E       A0,A2             IS OURS THERE?  @C@@@@          J         GETLDZ

)@@G@@@D@@@@          DSL       A2,36             SET FOR DIVIDE  @F@@@@      EE

)@@G@@  IOW$              READ THE LUT RECORD   @B@@@@          TZ,S1     LUTREK
)@@G@@D+3           OK? @B@@@@          SLJ       IOR               NO  @^@@@@EL
)@@G@@          ON        SNAP@ @@@@          LA,U      A0,LUTSNP @ @@@@      EM
)@@G@@    ER        SNAP$     @#@@@@          OFF     @G@@@@          LA      EN

)@@G@@LNK - INTERFACE FOR FORTRAN CALLS TO DIREC$ SUBROUTINES     @[@@@@.     ET

)@@G@@@F@@@@.   WILL RETURN WITH A0 POINTING TO USER'S PARAMETER LIST, AND    EV
)@@G@@@F@@@@.   LOWER X11 = NORMAL RETURN ADDRESS.  IF H1 OF A2 IS POSITIVE   EW
)@@G@@@F@@@@.   ON INPUT, THE ERROR RETURN ADDRESS WILL BE PUT IN UPPER X11.  EX
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @E@@@@FORLNK    LXI,U     X11,0             CLEAR ERROR RETUEY
)@@G@@RN    @F@@@@          TZ,S1     0,X11             IS THIS AN ASCII FTN CEZ
)@@G@@ALL   @G@@@@.                                     (OR 'T' SERIES FORTRANFA
)@@G@@-V WITH NO  @D@@@@.                                     ARGUMENTS) ?    FB

)@@G@@. NOW HAVE NORMAL RETURN ADDRESS IN LOWER X11, AND ADDRESS OF USER'S    FJ
)@@G@@@^@@@@. PARAMETER LIST IN A0. @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. NOTE - FOR 'T' SERIES FK
)@@G@@FORTRAN-V WITH NO ARGUMENTS, WE DON'T CARE@F@@@@.        ABOUT THE PARAMFL
)@@G@@ETER LIST, BUT A2 HAD BETTER BE NEGATIVE! @F@@@@.        ALSO, SINCE WE FM
)@@G@@USE 'FORPKT' TO INDICATE A FORTRAN CALL   @F@@@@.        (VS. ASSEMBLY),FN

)@@G@@Z,U     0,A0              'T' SERIES, NO ARGS, AND A0=0?    @H@@@@      FP

)@@G@@T OR TO     @D@@@@. THE NEW (MFDF) FORMAT, AND SET MFD$F ACCORDINGLY.   JX

)@@G@@R SPEC REMOTE TEST INSTRUCTION TABLE - CREATED BY INIT1, AND EXECUTED   CN
)@@G@@@^@@@@. BY 'CHECK' ROUTINE.   @[@@@@.     @E@@@@.     FOR SINGLE-WORD SPCO
)@@G@@ECS            FOR DOUBLE-WORD SPECS@E@@@@.     ---------------------   CP

)@@G@@@F@@@@SSLINK*   EQU       SSTAB+5           LINK TO POLISH TABLE ENTRY  DB
)@@G@@@E@@@@.                                     (FOR RESULT OF TEST)  @[@@@@DC
)@@G@@.     @G@@@@. POLISH: POLISH NOTATION TABLE.  INIT1 DECODES THE AND'S, ODD
)@@G@@R'S, AND    @G@@@@.         XOR'S INTO NUMBERS, AND PLACES THESE NUMBERSDE
)@@G@@ IN THE POLISH    @G@@@@.         TABLE IN THE ORDER IN WHICH THEY ARE EDF
)@@G@@NCOUNTERED.  A BLANK    @F@@@@.         ENTRY IS LEFT FOR EACH ACTUAL TEDG
)@@G@@ST SPEC WHICH IS FOUND, @G@@@@.         AND WHEN THE TEST IS PERFORMED, DH
)@@G@@THE RESULT IS PLACED IN THE   @C@@@@.         PROPER LOCATION IN THE POLDI
)@@G@@ISH TABLE.  @[@@@@.     @E@@@@POLISH*   RES       NSSP              POLIDJ
)@@G@@SH NOTATION TABLE @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. TRANS: THIS TABLE CONTAINS THE INTDK

)@@G@@OR SINGLE-FILE DREAD$ ? @E@@@@          AN,U      A0,1              YES,WS

)@@G@@  PR063             NO - SKIP @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. BIT 2**35 OF MI0+21 ISXP
)@@G@@ USED TO INDICATE 800-FPI MODE FOR DUAL-  @E@@@@. DENSITY 9-TRACK MSA TAXQ
)@@G@@PE DRIVES.  IT IS SET FOR 800, CLEAR@E@@@@. FOR 1600.  THIS IS THE ONLY XR
)@@G@@WAY TO CHECK FOR 'V' OPTION.  @E@@@@. HOWEVER, THIS BIT IS CLEAR FOR 7-TXS
)@@G@@RACK MSA DRIVES, SO WE  @F@@@@. MUST CHECK FOR 9-TRACK BEFORE ADDING THEXT
)@@G@@ 'V'.  I DON'T LIKE     @D@@@@. THIS, SINCE IT RELIES ON THE 'OLD EQUIPMXU

)@@G@@@[@@@@/.    @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. CONTINUATION OF 'PCTDAD' SUBROUTINE.  FILY
)@@G@@NDS NEXT DAD/GRANULE ITEM     @E@@@@. (FOR A PARTICULAR FILE) IN THE PCTLZ
)@@G@@, AND RETURNS IT TO THE @F@@@@. CALLER IN MI0.  THE ONLY CALLER AT THE TMA
)@@G@@IME OF THIS WRITING     @F@@@@. IS THE 'PRINT' ROUTINE, WHICH USES IT TOMB
)@@G@@ SNAP THE DAD/GTB OF    @#@@@@. TEMPORARY FILES.@[@@@@.     @F@@@@PCTDADMC

)@@G@@    LXI,U     A0,1              SET INC FOR BT  @F@@@@          LXM,U   MN
)@@G@@  A1,MI0            SET BT DESTINATION AS MI0   @D@@@@          LXI,U   MO

)@@G@@  DO THE TRANSFER @E@@@@          LX,U      X10,1,X10         SET TO RETMR
)@@G@@URN TO 1,X10@E@@@@.                                     FALL THRU TO PCTMS

)@@G@@    ON        (CHKPCT>0)**(LDJOK=0) @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. THIS SUBROUTINE PY
)@@G@@IS FOR USE WHEN LDJ OF PCT BANK IS NOT DESIRED  @F@@@@. (LDJOK EQU 0).  PZ

)@@G@@  DEFINE CONFIGURATION PARAMETERS   @D@@@@          EQUFS     .         SS
)@@G@@        DEFINE TAGS     @ @@@@          ON        SORTOK    @E@@@@NREC  ST
)@@G@@    +         NFILES/2          NUMBER OF RECORDS     @E@@@@NCHAR     + SU
)@@G@@        RECCHAR           CHARACTERS PER RECORD @[@@@@.     @B@@@@$(1). SV
)@@G@@CALL SORTF TO ASSIGN SORT FILES     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@OPNSRT*   SR      SW
)@@G@@  R15,SORTED        MARK SORT-SEG-LOADED  @E@@@@          LA,U      A0,NSX
)@@G@@FILES         GET NUMBER OF FILES   @G@@@@          TZ        ZPT       SY
)@@G@@        PRIVILEGED AND DOING EVERYTHING?  @F@@@@          SA        A0,NSZ
)@@G@@REC           YES, BETTER INCREASE NREC   @D@@@@          DO        SRTDTA
)@@G@@BG , P$RINT (0101,('SORTF ')) @E@@@@          LMJ       X11,SORTF       TB
)@@G@@  ASSIGN SORT FILES     @E@@@@          +         NREC              NUMBTC
)@@G@@ER OF RECORDS     @F@@@@          +         NCHAR             NUMBER OF TD
)@@G@@CHAR PER RECORD   @B@@@@          +         0                 WB  @F@@@@TE
)@@G@@NOSORTF*  R$OPN     SORTBL            OPEN SORT, RETURN TO FPOC   @F@@@@TF
)@@G@@. DON'T NEED PARAMETER CARD PROCESSING, SO REPLACE KPARCD WITH:   @[@@@@TG
)@@G@@.     @ @@@@ROPN$*    LMJ       X1,RSTRG$ @#@@@@          'ROPN$ '@ @@@@TH
)@@G@@          J         RBPN$     @]@@@@RTMIN$*   . @]@@@@RTMAX$*   . @]@@@@TI
)@@G@@RTPT$*    . @]@@@@RTST$*    . @]@@@@RTMT$*    . @]@@@@RLBLK$*   . @[@@@@TJ
)@@G@@.     @^@@@@. RELEASE RECORD TO SORT@[@@@@.     @]@@@@GOTREC*   . @G@@@@TK
)@@G@@          SA        BACKEDUP,SAVEBAK  SAVE RDISC AND BACKED-UP FLAGS    TL
)@@G@@@A@@@@          SA        RDISC,SAVERDISC @D@@@@          DO        SRTDTM
)@@G@@BG , P$RINT (0101,('RREL$ ')) @E@@@@          L,U       A0,RECSTART     TN
)@@G@@  PASS THIS FILE TO SORT@^@@@@          R$REL     .   @G@@@@          J TO
)@@G@@        CHK000            GET NEXT FILE (SEG IS LOADED)     @[@@@@.     TP
)@@G@@@B@@@@. DIRSEC EOF HAS OCCURRED; DO THE SORT    @[@@@@.     @]@@@@DOSORTTQ
)@@G@@*   . @D@@@@          DO        SRTDBG , P$RINT (0101,('RSORT$')) @F@@@@TR
)@@G@@          R$SORT    .                 DO THE SORT, RETURN TO LPOC @]@@@@TS
)@@G@@LPOC*     . @D@@@@          DO        SRTDBG , P$RINT (0101,('LPOC  ')) TT
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @F@@@@. GET NEXT RECORD FROM SORT, AND JUMP TO PRINT ROUTINETU
)@@G@@ WITH IT    @[@@@@.     @]@@@@SRTNXT*   . @D@@@@          DO        SRTDTV
)@@G@@BG , P$RINT (0101,('RRET$ ')) @H@@@@          R$RET     SRTEOF          TW
)@@G@@. GET NEXT RECORD - IF EOF, GO TO SRTEOF  @F@@@@          LX,U      X8,,TX
)@@G@@A0            POINT TO LI0/MI0/MI1 ETC.   @F@@@@          LA        BACKTY
)@@G@@EDUP,SAVEBAK  RETRIEVE RDISC, BAK FLAGS   @A@@@@          LA        RDISTZ
)@@G@@C,SAVERDISC @D@@@@          LA        FILESIZE,SAVESIZE RETRIEVE SIZE   UA
)@@G@@@H@@@@          J         PR000             JUMP TO PRINT ROUTINE (SEG IUB
)@@G@@S LOADED)   @[@@@@.     @A@@@@. EOF STATUS RECEIVED FROM SORT     @[@@@@UC
)@@G@@.     @E@@@@SRTEOF    TNZ       SFMODE2           SINGLE-FILE MODE?     UD
)@@G@@@E@@@@          J         MFD600            NO, RETURN TO MAIN SEG@F@@@@UE
)@@G@@          J         QF900             YES, RETURN FOR ANOTHER FILE@ @@@@UF
)@@G@@          OFF       SORTOK    @#@@@@          END     ___ERS PER RECORD UG
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @B@@@@$(1). CALL SORTF TO ASSIGN SOR*[S@@@*SDFF*@^@@@@      UH
)@@G@@    AXR$      .   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@.         SORTF - FORTRAN CALLABLE RUI
)@@G@@OUTINE TO ASSIGN SORT FILES   @[@@@@.     @B@@@@.         ORIGINALLY BY UJ
)@@G@@WALT GILBERT (UOM)@D@@@@.         UPDATED BY R. DUFF KURLAND (ISD) TO PRUK
)@@G@@OVIDE:@[@@@@.     @B@@@@.           - EXEC LEVEL 33 COMPATABILITY @C@@@@UL
)@@G@@.           - REMOVABLE DISC USAGE FOR XB FILE  @[@@@@.     @H@@@@.     UM
)@@G@@    IF AN 'XB' FILE IS NEEDED, IT WILL BE ASSIGNED ON TYPE <FIXTYPE>,   UN
)@@G@@@G@@@@.         UNLESS THE MAXIMUM DRUM FILE SIZE (XBMAXF) IS EXCEEDED, UO
)@@G@@OR THE@H@@@@.         REQUIRED NUMBER OF POSITIONS EXCEEDS THE AMOUNT CUUP
)@@G@@RRENTLY AVAILABLE.@G@@@@.         IN THIS CASE, 'XB' WILL BE ASSIGNED ONUQ
)@@G@@ A REMOVABLE DISC, USING@H@@@@.         EQUIPMENT TYPE <REMTYPE>, AND PAUR
)@@G@@CKID <REMPACK>.  IF NO REMOVABLE    @G@@@@.         DISC ASSIGNS ARE DESUS
)@@G@@IRED, <REMTYPE> SHOULD BE SET TO ZERO.    @[@@@@.     @H@@@@.         IFUT
)@@G@@ A REMOVABLE ASSIGN OF 'XB' IS ATTEMPTED AND FAILS (DUE TO THE    @G@@@@UU
)@@G@@.         DRIVE NOT BEING AVAILABLE, ETC.), SORTF WILL REVERT TO A FIXEDUV
)@@G@@@H@@@@.         ASSIGN, BUT WITHOUT THE INITIAL RESERVE.  FURTHERMORE, IUW
)@@G@@F THE FILE  @H@@@@.         IS LESS THAN <XBREVP> POSITIONS, TRACK GRANUUX
)@@G@@LARITY WILL BE USED.    @G@@@@.         THIS IS ALL TO MINIMIZE THE SYSTUY
)@@G@@EM IMPACT OF A SORT WHEN MASS @B@@@@.         STORAGE AVAILABILITY IS LOUZ
)@@G@@W.    @[@@@@.     @F@@@@REMTYPE   EQU       0                 TYPE FOR RVA
)@@G@@EMOVABLE XB ASGS  @E@@@@.                                     MUST BE 3 VB
)@@G@@CHARS, RJSF @G@@@@FIXTYPE   EQU       'F40'             TYPE TO USE FOR VC
)@@G@@FIXED XB ASGS     @D@@@@.                                     (3 CHARS, VD
)@@G@@RJSF) @H@@@@REMPACK   EQU       'TEMP00'          PACKID FOR REMOVABLE XVE
)@@G@@B ASGS (LJSF)     @F@@@@.                                     IGNORED IFVF
)@@G@@ REMTYPE = 0.     @H@@@@XBMAXF    EQU       0                 MAX SIZE OVG
)@@G@@F FIXED XB FILE (POSITIONS)   @F@@@@.                                   VH
)@@G@@  IGNORED IF REMTYPE = 0.     @F@@@@XBMAX     EQU       150             VI
)@@G@@  MAX XB SIZE, ANY ASG TYPE   @F@@@@.                                   VJ
)@@G@@  (ONLY TO PREVENT ABUSE)     @F@@@@MSIZE     EQU       300             VK
)@@G@@  MSALL$ FATBL BUFFER SIZE    @[@@@@.     @C@@@@RTYPE     EQU       ('.,VL
)@@G@@'*/24)+(REMTYPE*/6)+'/' @C@@@@FTYPE     EQU       ('.,'*/24)+(FIXTYPE*/6VM
)@@G@@)+'/' @[@@@@.     @A@@@@.         ALL FILES ARE FREED FIRST @[@@@@.     VN
)@@G@@@^@@@@FREXA     '@FREE XA    '@^@@@@FREXB     '@FREE XB    '@^@@@@FRECORVO
)@@G@@    '@FREE R$CORE'@[@@@@.     @ @@@@.         XA FILE ASSIGN IMAGE@[@@@@VP
)@@G@@.     @A@@@@ASGXA     '@ASG,T    XA.,F///******'@ @@@@ASGXAL    EQU     VQ
)@@G@@  $-ASGXA   @[@@@@.     @A@@@@.         XB FILE ASSIGN IMAGES     @[@@@@VR
)@@G@@.     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         NORMAL (FIXED) XB ASSIGN, EXTENDED FORVS
)@@G@@ REMOVABLE ASSIGN IF    @A@@@@.         CONFIGURED AND NECESSARY. @[@@@@VT
)@@G@@.     @B@@@@ASGXB     '@ASG,T    XB.,FXX/***/POS/*** '@G@@@@ASGXBL    EQVU
)@@G@@U       $-ASGXB           LENGTH OF NORMAL XB ASSIGN IMAGE  @ @@@@      VV
)@@G@@    ON        REMTYPE   @H@@@@XBPACK    +         REMPACK           PACKVW
)@@G@@ID TAGGED ONTO END OF XB ASG IMAGE  @G@@@@DISC      +         0         VX
)@@G@@        NONZERO IF REMOVABLE ASG NEEDED   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@.         REVY
)@@G@@MOTE EXECUTE TABLE TO STUFF COMMA AFTER MAX GRANS     @[@@@@.     @F@@@@VZ
)@@G@@COMMA     S,S2      A0,ASGXB+4        FOR MAX = INITIAL = 1 DIGIT @F@@@@WA
)@@G@@          S,S4      A0,ASGXB+4        FOR MAX = INITIAL = 2 DIGITS@F@@@@WB
)@@G@@          S,S6      A0,ASGXB+4        FOR MAX = INITIAL = 3 DIGITS@[@@@@WC
)@@G@@.     @E@@@@.         XB ASSIGN IMAGE USED WHEN REMOVABLE ASSIGN FAILS. WD
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @B@@@@ASGXB2    '@ASG,T    XB.,FXX//POS/ ******'@ @@@@ASGXB2WE
)@@G@@L   EQU       $-ASGXB2  @[@@@@.     @G@@@@XBREVP    EQU       10        WF
)@@G@@        POINT AT WHICH TO STOP SWITCHING  @E@@@@.                       WG
)@@G@@              TO TRACK GRANULARITY  @ @@@@          OFF       REMTYPE   WH
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @ @@@@.         R$CORE ASSIGN IMAGE @[@@@@.     @A@@@@ASGCORWI
)@@G@@    '@ASG,T R$CORE.,F2///**  '@ @@@@ASGCORL   EQU       $-ASGCOR  @[@@@@WJ
)@@G@@.     @^@@@@.         MSALL$ PACKET @[@@@@.     @G@@@@MSPKT     +       WK
)@@G@@  1,MSALL$          LEVEL-33 FORMAT MSCON$/MSALL$ CALL@E@@@@          + WL
)@@G@@        MSIZE,MSBUF       BUFFER LENGTH, ADDRESS@D@@@@          +       WM
)@@G@@  0                 FILLED BY MSCON$@D@@@@          +         0         WN
)@@G@@        FILLED BY MSCON$@D@@@@          +         0                 FILLWO
)@@G@@ED BY MSCON$@[@@@@.     @F@@@@MSBEG     EQUF      MSPKT+3,,H1       STARWP
)@@G@@TING MS DEVICE INDEX    @E@@@@MSEND     EQUF      MSPKT+3,,H2       LASTWQ
)@@G@@ MS DEVICE INDEX  @F@@@@DSCBEG    EQUF      MSPKT+4,,H1       STARTING DWR
)@@G@@ISC DEVICE INDEX  @E@@@@DSCEND    EQUF      MSPKT+4,,H2       LAST DISC WS
)@@G@@DEVICE INDEX@[@@@@.     @ @@@@.         MSALL$ FATBL BUFFER @[@@@@.     WT
)@@G@@@F@@@@MSBUF     RES       MSIZE             RESERVE SPACE FOR FATBL     WU
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @E@@@@SAV       RES       1                 SAVE AREA FOR A1WV
)@@G@@0     @[@@@@.     @B@@@@E(1)      'RECORD SIZE NEGATIVE OR ZERO'. @C@@@@WW
)@@G@@E(2)      'NUMBER OF RECORDS NEGATIVE OR ZERO'. @D@@@@E(3)      'XXXXXX WX
)@@G@@POSITIONS IS TOO LARGE FOR SORTF'.  @E@@@@E(4)      'SORT FILE ASSIGN REWY
)@@G@@JECTED:    XXXXXXXXXXXX'.     @G@@@@E(5)      ' ONLY XXXXXX TRACKS OF STWZ
)@@G@@ORAGE  REMAIN,   SORT NEEDS  XXXXXX'@E@@@@E(6)      ' ONLY XXXXXX POSITIXA
)@@G@@ONS REMAIN, SORT NEEDS XXXXXX'@D@@@@E(7)      'SORTF ERROR - MSALL$ BUFFXB
)@@G@@ER IS TOO SMALL.' @B@@@@E(8)      'SORTF MSCON$ ERROR CODE XX'    @]@@@@XC
)@@G@@E(9)      . @^@@@@I         DO        8 ,;@F@@@@EE(I)     + 0200+E(I+1)-XD
)@@G@@E(I),E(I).    GENERATE PRINT CONTROL WORDS@F@@@@XA        +         0   XE
)@@G@@              XA (SMALL) FILE SIZE, TRK   @F@@@@XB        +         0   XF
)@@G@@              XB (LARGE) FILE SIZE, POS   @G@@@@CORE      +         0   XG
)@@G@@              CORE SIZE, THOUSANDS OF WORDS     @[@@@@.     @A@@@@.     XH
)@@G@@    MERGE POWER LLOKUP TABLE  @[@@@@.     @B@@@@MGPS      +         2   XI
)@@G@@              4   @B@@@@          +         5                 5   @B@@@@XJ
)@@G@@          +         9                 6   @B@@@@          +         17  XK
)@@G@@              7   @B@@@@          +         26                8   @B@@@@XL
)@@G@@          +         37                9   @B@@@@          +         53  XM
)@@G@@              10  @B@@@@          +         72                11  @B@@@@XN
)@@G@@          +         94                12  @B@@@@          +         121 XO
)@@G@@              13  @B@@@@          +         153               14  @B@@@@XP
)@@G@@          +         190               15  @B@@@@          +         232 XQ
)@@G@@              16  @B@@@@          +         280               17  @B@@@@XR
)@@G@@          +         335               18  @B@@@@          +         395 XS
)@@G@@              19  @B@@@@          +         460               20  @B@@@@XT
)@@G@@          +         530               21  @F@@@@NMGPS     EQU       $-MGXU
)@@G@@PS.           NUMBER OF ENTRIES IN TABLE  @[@@@@.     @F@@@@RETURN    + XV
)@@G@@        0                 RETURN ADDRESS STORE HERE   @[@@@@/$(1).@]@@@@XW
)@@G@@SORTF*    . @ @@@@          S         A10,SAV   @G@@@@          L,U     XX
)@@G@@  A1,'WJG'          LOAD @SORTF CALL IDENTITY FLAG    @H@@@@          SZXY
)@@G@@        A4                SET FLAG. 0=SUBROUTINE CALL, _0=@SORTF  @G@@@@XZ
)@@G@@          TNE,H2    A1,2,X11          IS THIS SORTF-DRIVER CALLING?     YA
)@@G@@@H@@@@          L         A4,2,X11          YES, LOAD ENTIRE WORD TO GETYB
)@@G@@ SIGN FLAG  @H@@@@          JN        A4,NOCSF          DON'T ISSUE CSF$YC
)@@G@@'S IF 'X' OPTION ON     @H@@@@          L         A0,(2,FREXA)      FREEYD
)@@G@@ ALL OF THE FILES: XA, XB, R$CORE   @^@@@@          ER        CSF$@A@@@@YE
)@@G@@          L         A0,(2,FREXB)    @^@@@@          ER        CSF$@A@@@@YF
)@@G@@          L         A0,(2,FRECOR)   @^@@@@          ER        CSF$@E@@@@YG
)@@G@@NOCSF     L,U       A0,3,X11          GET RETURN ADDRESS    @C@@@@      YH
)@@G@@    S,H2      A0,RETURN         SAVE IT.  @F@@@@          L         A1,*YI
)@@G@@1,X11         LOAD RECORD SIZE IN CHARS   @E@@@@          JN        A1,EYJ
)@@G@@RR2           ERROR IF NEGATIVE     @ @@@@          A,U       A1,11 .   YK
)@@G@@@^@@@@          SZ        A0  @E@@@@          DI,U      A0,6            YL
)@@G@@  CONVERT TO WORD COUNT @F@@@@          MSI       A0,*0,X11         TIMEYM
)@@G@@S NUMBER OF RECORDS     @E@@@@          JN        A0,ERR1           ERROYN
)@@G@@R IF NEGATIVE     @E@@@@          MI,U      A0,11             ADD 10% SAYO
)@@G@@FETY FACTOR @ @@@@          DI,U      A0,10     @ @@@@          DSL     YP
)@@G@@  A0,36     @D@@@@          S         A1,A2             SAVE VALUE.     YQ
)@@G@@@E@@@@          DI,U      A0,114688         GET FILE SIZE IN POS  @F@@@@YR
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,SMALL          JUMP IF LESS THAN 1 POSITION@D@@@@YS
)@@G@@          A,U       A0,1              ROUND UPWARD    @F@@@@          S YT
)@@G@@        A0,XB             STORE XB SIZE, POSITIONS    @E@@@@          TGYU
)@@G@@,U      A0,XBMAX+1        MAX XB SIZE EXCEEDED? @E@@@@          J       YV
)@@G@@  ERR3              YES, PRINT ERROR MSG  @F@@@@          L,U       R1,NYW
)@@G@@MGPS          SEARCH MERGE-POWER TABLE    @ @@@@          L         A2,(YX
)@@G@@1,3)  @H@@@@          SG,H2     A0,MGPS-3,*A2     LOOKUP XB SIZE IN MERGYY
)@@G@@E-POWER TABLE     @D@@@@          J         ERR3              MUCH TOO BYZ
)@@G@@IG!   @G@@@@          L,U       A1,0,A2           RESULT, MGP (MERGE-POWZA
)@@G@@ER) IN A2   @H@@@@          MSI,U     A1,1792           FIND AMOUNT OF CZB
)@@G@@ORE USING 1792-WD BUFFER@G@@@@          A,U       A1,2791           2791ZC
)@@G@@=1792+999 = 1TRK + ROUNDING   @^@@@@          SZ        A0  @ @@@@      ZD
)@@G@@    DI,U      A0,1000   @F@@@@          S         A0,CORE           COREZE
)@@G@@ REQUIRED IN THOUSANDS. @H@@@@          MI,U      A0,15000          15 (ZF
)@@G@@1.5) IS DEFAULT BIAS, 1000 TO GET WD@H@@@@          AN,U      A1,80640  ZG
)@@G@@        CALC. EXPECTED STRING SIZE,  3*15*1792  @H@@@@          DI,U    ZH
)@@G@@  A0,19712          11*1792 TO GET TRKS, 11 = 10 ALMOST     @C@@@@      ZI
)@@G@@    S         A0,A3             SAVE VALUE@E@@@@          L         A0,XZJ
)@@G@@B             NOW CALCULATE XA SIZE @E@@@@          DSL       A0,30     ZK
)@@G@@        (CONV POS TO TRK)     @H@@@@          DI,U      A0,0,A2         ZL
)@@G@@  XA = XB/(MGP)+1 ROUNDED UP TO STRING SIZ@H@@@@          AU        A0,AZM
)@@G@@3             NOW ROUND UP TO WHOLE EXPECTED ST. SIZE.@^@@@@          SZZN
)@@G@@        A0  @ @@@@          DI        A0,A3     @ @@@@          MSI     ZO
)@@G@@  A0,A3     @E@@@@          S         A0,XA             STORE XA SIZE, TZP
)@@G@@RKS   @ @@@@          ON        REMTYPE   @F@@@@          L         A0,XZQ
)@@G@@B             LOAD XB SIZE, IN POSITIONS  @F@@@@          TLE,U     A0,XZR
)@@G@@BMAXF+1       MAX FIXED POS EXCEEDED?     @F@@@@          J         MAVCZS
)@@G@@HK            NO, CHECK MS AVAILABILITY   @F@@@@DISCON    L,U       A0,1ZT
)@@G@@              YES, SET REMOVABLE ASG FLAG @ @@@@          S         A0,DZU
)@@G@@ISC   @G@@@@          J         CHEKD             TRY ASSIGNING XB ON REZV
)@@G@@MOBAVLE PACK@ @@@@          OFF       REMTYPE   @C@@@@MAVCHK    L,U     ZW
)@@G@@  A0,MSPKT          GET FATBL @ @@@@          ER        MSCON$    @F@@@@ZX
)@@G@@          JN        A0,ERR7           IF NO GOOD, HANDLE ERROR    @F@@@@ZY
)@@G@@          SZ        A10               CLEAR TOTAL TRACKS AVAILABLE@G@@@@ZZ
)@@G@@          SZ        A1                CLEAR TOTAL POSITIONS AVAILLABLE  AA
)@@G@@@F@@@@          L         A2,MSEND          GET LAST MS DEVICE INDEX    AB
)@@G@@@E@@@@          AN        A2,MSBEG          GET # OF MS TYPES - 1 @D@@@@AC
)@@G@@          TNZ       MSBEG             NEW-TYPE FATBL? @F@@@@          L,AD
)@@G@@U       A2,7              NO, GET OLD LENGTH OF FATBL @F@@@@FATLOOP   L,AE
)@@G@@H1      A0,MSBUF,A2       GET INDEX TO STATUS TABLE   @D@@@@          TNAF
)@@G@@Z       MSBEG             NEW-TYPE FATBL? @F@@@@          JZ        A0,FAG
)@@G@@ATEND         NO, IF ZERO, NONE CONFIGURED@F@@@@          A,H2      A1,MAH
)@@G@@SBUF+2,A0     BUMP AVAILABLE POSITIONS    @E@@@@          L         A0,MAI
)@@G@@SBUF+1,A0     GET POSITIONS AVAIL   @F@@@@          LSSL      A0,12     AJ
)@@G@@        GET RID OF  ROT POINTER     @ @@@@          SSL       A0,12     AK
)@@G@@@E@@@@          A         A10,A0            BUMP AVAILABLE TRACKS @E@@@@AL
)@@G@@FATEND    JGD       A2,FATLOOP        HANDLE ALL MS DEVICES @G@@@@      AM
)@@G@@    TLE       A1,XB             ENOUGH POSITIONS FOR THE XB FILE? @E@@@@AN
)@@G@@          DO REMTYPE=0 , J ERR6       NO, PRINT ERROR MSG   @F@@@@      AO
)@@G@@    DO REMTYPE>0 , J DISCON     NO, SWITCH TO REMOVABLE ASG @F@@@@      AP
)@@G@@    L         A1,XB             GET POSITIONS NEEDED FOR XB @E@@@@      AQ
)@@G@@    LSSL      A1,6              CONVERT TO TRACKS     @F@@@@          A AR
)@@G@@        A1,XA             ADD TRACKS REQUIRED FOR XA  @B@@@@          A,AS
)@@G@@U       A1,1248           ??? @F@@@@          TLE       A10,A1          AT
)@@G@@  ARE ENOUGH TRACKS AVAILABLE?@E@@@@          J         ERR5            AU
)@@G@@  NO, PRINT ERROR MSG   @[@@@@.     @ @@@@.         ASSIGN THE XB FILE  AV
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @ @@@@CHEKD     L         A0,XB     @F@@@@          JZ      AW
)@@G@@  A0,CVXA           SKIP IF NO XB FILE NEEDED   @F@@@@          LMJ     AX
)@@G@@  X11,CV            CONVERT TO FIELDATA DECIMAL @^@@@@          SZ      AY
)@@G@@  A0  @ @@@@          L         A1,A2     @E@@@@          LDSL      A0,0AZ
)@@G@@,A3           MOVE INIT RESV TO A0  @A@@@@          L         A1,('/POS/BA
)@@G@@ ')   @G@@@@          DSL       A0,6              MOVE LAST CHAR OF INITBB
)@@G@@ RESV TO A1 @G@@@@          AN,U      A3,6              DECREMENT SHIFT BC
)@@G@@COUNT BY 1 CHAR   @F@@@@          DSL       A1,0,A3           SHIFT X/POBD
)@@G@@S/ AND MAX GRAN   @H@@@@          SSC       A0,0,A3           ADJUST REMBE
)@@G@@AINING CHARS OF INIT RESV     @G@@@@          A         A1,A0           BF
)@@G@@  ADD REMAINING INIT RESV CHARS     @G@@@@          DS        A1,ASGXB+3BG
)@@G@@        STORE XXX/POS/XXX IN ASG IMAGE    @F@@@@          LA        A0,(BH
)@@G@@FTYPE)        GET FIXED XB EQUIP TYPE     @E@@@@          SA        A0,ABI
)@@G@@SGXB+2        STORE IN ASG IMAGE    @E@@@@          L         A1,(ASGXBLBJ
)@@G@@,ASGXB) GET IMAGE LENGTH, ADDR@ @@@@          ON        REMTYPE   @F@@@@BK
)@@G@@          TNZ       DISC              AH!  SHOULD WE DO REM ASG?  @E@@@@BL
)@@G@@          J         DOIT              NO, ASSIGN AS FIXED   @F@@@@      BM
)@@G@@    L         A2,(RTYPE)        GET DESIRED REM EQUIP TYPE  @E@@@@      BN
)@@G@@    S         A2,ASGXB+2        STORE IN ASG IMAGE    @[@@@@.     @B@@@@BO
)@@G@@.         ADD A COMMA FOR PACKID CLAUSE   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@          SZBP
)@@G@@        A2                A3=INIT RESV BIT COUNT - 6  @E@@@@          DIBQ
)@@G@@,U      A2,6              CONVERT TO CHAR COUNT @D@@@@          L,U     BR
)@@G@@  A0,','            GET A COMMA     @F@@@@          EX        COMMA,A2  BS
)@@G@@        STORE COMMA IN ASG IMAGE    @G@@@@          LNA       A1,(ASGXBLBT
)@@G@@+1,ASGXB) . INDICATE WE CHECK THE STATUS  @ @@@@          OFF       REMTBU
)@@G@@YPE   @[@@@@.     @E@@@@DOIT      LMJ       A3,ISSUE          ASSIGN THEBV
)@@G@@ XB FILE    @ @@@@          ON        REMTYPE   @D@@@@          JP      BW
)@@G@@  A0,CVXA           IF OK, GO ASG XA@E@@@@          TNZ       DISC      BX
)@@G@@        WAS THIS A DISC ASG?  @F@@@@          J         ISSUE3          BY
)@@G@@  NO, PRINT ERROR MSG AND EXIT@[@@@@.     @F@@@@.         MAYBE PACK CANBZ
)@@G@@'T BE MOUNTED.  REVERT TO FIXED ASSIGN,   @E@@@@.         WITHOUT INITIACA
)@@G@@L RESERVE.  IF FILE IS SMALL ENOUGH @F@@@@.         (LESS THAN <XBREVP> CB

)@@G@@  A4,SKIPIT         IF NOT SORTF-DRIVER, SKIP MSG     @D@@@@          LMCD

)@@G@@  RETURN TO CALLING PROGRAM   @[@@@@.     @D@@@@.         SUBROUTINE TO DG
)@@G@@DISPLAY AND ISSUE CSF$ REQUEST@[@@@@.     @H@@@@.         ENTER WITH A1 DH
)@@G@@= IMAGE LENGTH,ADDRESS   OR   -(IMAGE LENGTH,ADDRESS) @H@@@@.         A1DI
)@@G@@ NEGATIVE INDICATES THAT CALLER WISHES TO CHECK STATUS HIMSELF.   @[@@@@DJ

)@@G@@        ERR4B             PRINT IT AND EXIT     @[@@@@.     @A@@@@.     DV

)@@G@@0')   @C@@@@          JZ        A0,ERR4A          DONE?     @E@@@@      EA

)@@G@@@D@@@@          J         0,A3              RETURN TO CALLER@[@@@@.     ED

)@@G@@        PRINT ERROR MSG @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         BINARY TO FIELDATA DEF
)@@G@@ECIMAL CONVERSION ROUTINE:  INPUT IN A0,  @H@@@@.         OUTPUT LEFT-JUEG
)@@G@@STIFIED, SPACE FILLED IN A2.  A3 = CHAR COUNT * 6.    @[@@@@.     @H@@@@EH

)@@G@@CC!@@]>8)@@K/K@@HNG8K@@J*[S@@@*SDFF*@F@@@@. @MFD SNAP$ ROUTINE - DUMPS DSS
)@@G@@IRECTORY ITEMS SELECTED BY THE USER @[@@@@.     @^@@@@          AXR$    ST
)@@G@@  .   @G@@@@          CONFIG    .                 DEFINE CONFIGURATION PSU

)@@G@@  .                 DEFINE TAGS     @D@@@@PRT       FORM      12,6,18   SW
)@@G@@        FORM T1,S3,H2   @[@@@@.     @^@@@@P         PROC      1   @^@@@@SX
)@@G@@SNAPP*    NAME      0   @^@@@@SETSNAP*  NAME      1   @F@@@@          DOSY
)@@G@@ P(1)=0 , GO ERONLY       SKIP IF NO PARAMETERS GIVEN @D@@@@          LASZ
)@@G@@        A0,(P(1,1))       GET HEADER INFO @H@@@@          DO OLDMFD=0 , TA
)@@G@@GO ON         SKIP 'DAD' CHECK IF NEW FORMAT ONLY     @E@@@@       DO 1-TB
)@@G@@(P(1,1)='DAD   ') , GO ON SKIP IF NOT 'DAD'     @E@@@@          TNZ     TC
)@@G@@  MFD$F             NEW FORMAT DIRECTORY? @G@@@@          LA        A0,(TD
)@@G@@'GTB   ')     NO, USE 'GTB' RATHER THAN 'DAD'   @^@@@@ON        NAME    TE
)@@G@@  .   @E@@@@          SA        A0,SNAPKT         STORE IN SNAP$ PACKET TF
)@@G@@@E@@@@          LA,U      A0,P(1,2)         GET BUFFER ADDRESS    @F@@@@TG
)@@G@@          SA        A0,BUFAD          STORE IT IN SNAP$ PACKET    @H@@@@TH
)@@G@@          DO P(1)<3 , GO ERONLY       IF NOT SPECIFIED, LEAVE # WORDS ASTI
)@@G@@ IS   @F@@@@          LA,U      A0,P(1,3)         BUT IF SPECIFIED, USE TJ
)@@G@@IT    @E@@@@          SA        A0,NWRDS          SET # OF WORDS TO SNAPTK
)@@G@@@^@@@@ERONLY    NAME      .   @G@@@@          DO P(0,0)>0 , GO AWAY     TL
)@@G@@  SKIP IF JUST SETTING UP PACKET    @ @@@@          ON        SNAPSUB=0 TM
)@@G@@@F@@@@          LA,U      A0,SNAPKT         GET SNAP$ PACKET ADDRESS    TN
)@@G@@@D@@@@          ER        SNAP$             DO THE SNAP$    @ @@@@      TO
)@@G@@    OFF       SNAPSUB=0 @ @@@@          ON        SNAPSUB   @D@@@@      TP
)@@G@@    LMJ       X10,SNAP$         DO THE SNAP$    @D@@@@          LA      TQ
)@@G@@  A2,SNAP           RELOAD SNAP BITS@ @@@@          OFF       SNAPSUB   TR
)@@G@@@G@@@@          SR        R15,SNAPKT+2      SET SNAPPED-SOMETHING INDICATS
)@@G@@TOR   @C@@@@          DO (P(1,1)='LI0')++(P(1,1)='LI1') , ; @F@@@@      TT
)@@G@@    SR        R15,LISNPD        SET LEAD-ITEM-SNAPPED FLAG  @^@@@@AWAY  TU
)@@G@@    NAME      .   @#@@@@          END     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@SNAPKT    'STV
)@@G@@EC   '                    SNAP$ PACKET    @D@@@@          +         28,0TW
)@@G@@              ASSUME 1 SECTOR @^@@@@          +         0   @E@@@@NWRDS TX

)@@G@@    P$RINT    ( PRT 1,0,0)      SKIP A LINE     @G@@@@          L$OAD   ZY
)@@G@@  INSEG,IN2020,1    RETURN TO INITIALIZATION SEGMENT  @ @@@@          OFZZ
)@@G@@F       POLDBG    @ @@@@/         ON        SNAPSUB   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@AA
)@@G@@. THIS SUBROUTINE PEFORMS A MORE READABLE SNAP$-TYPE DUMP THAN IS @G@@@@AB
)@@G@@. AVAILABLE THROUGH ER SNAP$.  IT INCLUDES A SHORTER FORMAT FOR DEMAND  AC
)@@G@@@H@@@@. USE.  THIS ROUTINE IS USED ONLY IF CONFIG PARAMETER 'SNAPSUB' ISAD
)@@G@@ NONZERO.   @[@@@@.     @A@@@@.    ENTER VIA:  LMJ  X10,SNAP$     @G@@@@AE
)@@G@@.     DESTROYS:  X4, X10, X11, A6, R2, R4, PLUS REGISTERS USED BY EDIT$ AF
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @]@@@@$(0)      . @ @@@@ENTIRE    'ALL & WORDS = &'   @G@@@@AG
)@@G@@LASTWD    RES       1                 LAST WORD OF EACH LINE IS STORED  AH
)@@G@@@E@@@@.                                     HERE FOR COMPARISON   @E@@@@AI
)@@G@@WPL       RES       1                 # OF WORDS PER LINE   @[@@@@.     AJ
)@@G@@@F@@@@SLEN      EQU       5                 WORDS/LINE FOR SHORT LISTINGAK
)@@G@@@F@@@@LLEN      EQU       8                 WORDS/LINE FOR LONG LISTING AL
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @]@@@@$(1),SNAP$. @E@@@@          P$RINT    ( PRT 2,1,SNAPKTAM
)@@G@@) PRINT SNAP HEADER     @F@@@@          LA        A0,NWRDS          GET AN
)@@G@@NUMBER OF WORDS TO SNAP @F@@@@          AND,U     A0,077777         MASKAO
)@@G@@ OF XAR BITS TO BE SAFE @F@@@@          JZ        A1,,X10           IF NAP
)@@G@@O WORDS TO SNAP, RETURN @G@@@@          SA        A1,NWRDS          OTHEAQ
)@@G@@RWISE, PUT MASKED # WORDS BACK@E@@@@          LX        X4,(1,0)        AR
)@@G@@  INITIALIZE WORD INDEX @E@@@@          AX        X4,BUFAD          ADD AS
)@@G@@BUFFER ADDRESS    @G@@@@          TLE,U     A1,4              IF ONLY 1-AT
)@@G@@3 WORDS BEING SNAPPED,  @F@@@@          J         NOTSAM               SAU
)@@G@@KIP ALL-THE-SAME TEST   @F@@@@          AN,U      A1,1              MINUAV
)@@G@@S 1 FOR SEARCH COUNT    @D@@@@          SA        A1,R1             SET AW
)@@G@@SEARCH COUNT@H@@@@          LX        A2,X4             COPY WORD INDEX AX
)@@G@@AND INCREMENT TO A2     @E@@@@          LA        A0,0,A2           GET AY
)@@G@@1ST WORD OF AREA  @F@@@@          SNE       A0,1,*A2          FIND ANY DAZ
)@@G@@IFFERENT WORDS?   @D@@@@          J         $+2               NO, ALL THBA
)@@G@@E SAME@E@@@@          J         NOTSAM            YES, NOT ALL THE SAME BB
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @D@@@@. THE ENTIRE AREA IS EQUAL:  PRINT MESSAGE AND RETURN BC
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @C@@@@          E$DIT     EDPACK            OPEN EDIT @C@@@@BD
)@@G@@          E$MSG     ENTIRE            START MSG @E@@@@          E$DECV  BE
)@@G@@  NWRDS             EDIT NUMBER OF WORDS  @D@@@@          E$MSGR    .   BF
)@@G@@              CONTINUE MSG    @C@@@@          E$OCTV    0,X4            BG
)@@G@@  ADD VALUE @C@@@@          P$RINT    POUT              PRINT MSG @C@@@@BH
)@@G@@          J         0,X10             RETURN    @[@@@@.     @D@@@@. ENTIBI
)@@G@@RE AREA IS NOT EQUAL:  DUMP IT LINE BY LINE     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@NOTSAMBJ
)@@G@@    LA        A0,( PRT 1,0,0)   GET SET TO SKIP A LINE@D@@@@          TZBK
)@@G@@        LONGLIST          LONG LISTING?   @C@@@@          ER        PRINBL
)@@G@@T$            YES, DO IT@E@@@@          LA        A0,NWRDS          GET BM
)@@G@@# OF WORDS TO SNAP@E@@@@          DSL       A0,36             GET SET FOBN
)@@G@@R DIVIDE    @E@@@@          LA,U      A2,SLEN           GET SHORT WORDS/BO
)@@G@@LINE  @D@@@@          TZ        LONGLIST          LONG LISTING?   @F@@@@BP
)@@G@@          LA,U      A2,LLEN           YES, GET LONG WORDS/LINE    @E@@@@BQ
)@@G@@          SA        A2,WPL            STORE WORDS PER LINE  @F@@@@      BR
)@@G@@    DI        A0,A2             CALCULATE # OF LINES NEEDED @F@@@@      BS
)@@G@@    TZ        A1                REMAINDER ON PARTIAL LINE?  @B@@@@      BT
)@@G@@    AA,U      A0,1              YES @D@@@@          ANA,U     A0,1      BU
)@@G@@        ADJUST FOR JGD  @D@@@@          SA        A0,R4             SET BV
)@@G@@LOOP COUNT  @F@@@@          LA,U      A6,0              INITIALIZE SKIP BW
)@@G@@INDICATOR   @F@@@@          J         PRINTLINE         ALWAYS PRINT FIRBX
)@@G@@ST LINE     @[@@@@.     @H@@@@. BEFORE PRINTING EACH LINE (EXCEPT THE FIBY
)@@G@@RST AND LAST LINES), CHECK TO SEE   @H@@@@. IF ALL WORDS ON THIS LINE ARBZ
)@@G@@E EQUAL TO THE LAST WORD OF THE PREVIOUS LINE.  @H@@@@. IF SO, DO NOT PRCA
)@@G@@INT THIS LINE, BUT INDICATE, VIA A '*' ON THE NEXT PRINTED  @C@@@@. LINECB
)@@G@@, THAT AT LEAST ONE LINE HAS BEEN SKIPPED.@[@@@@.     @D@@@@LINELOOP  LACC
)@@G@@        A0,R4             GET LINE NUMBER @F@@@@          JZ        A0,PCD
)@@G@@RINTLINE      IF LAST LINE, DON'T SKIP IT @F@@@@          LR        R1,WCE
)@@G@@PL            GET # OF WORDS PER LINE     @G@@@@          LA        A0,LCF
)@@G@@ASTWD         GET LAST WORD FROM PREVIOUS LINE  @H@@@@          LX      CG
)@@G@@  A1,X4             COPY CURRENT INDEX AND INCREMENT TO A1  @G@@@@      CH
)@@G@@    SNE       A0,0,*A1          ANYTHING DIFFERENT ON THIS LINE?  @E@@@@CI
)@@G@@          J         $+2               NO, SKIP THIS LINE    @E@@@@      CJ
)@@G@@    J         PRINTLINE         YES, PRINT THIS LINE  @E@@@@          LACK
)@@G@@,U      A6,1              SET SKIP INDICATOR    @E@@@@          AX      CL
)@@G@@  X4,WPL            POINT TO NEXT LINE    @D@@@@          J         NEXTCM
)@@G@@LINE          SKIP THIS LINE  @[@@@@.     @E@@@@. WE DON'T WANT TO SKIP CN
)@@G@@THIS LINE:  COMPOSE AND PRINT IT    @[@@@@.     @C@@@@PRINTLINE E$DIT   CO
)@@G@@  EDPACK            OPEN EDIT @F@@@@          LR        R2,A6           CP
)@@G@@  HOLD PREVIOUS SKIP INDICATOR@F@@@@          LA,U      A6,0            CQ
)@@G@@  CLEAR NEW SKIP INDICATOR    @G@@@@          LA,U      A0,0,X4         CR
)@@G@@  GET INDEX OF FIRST WORD IN LINE   @E@@@@          ANA       A0,BUFAD  CS
)@@G@@        MAKE IT RELATIVE TO 0 @D@@@@          E$OCTF    4               CT
)@@G@@  EDIT THE NUMBER @D@@@@          E$SKIP    1                 SKIP A SPACU
)@@G@@CE    @E@@@@          LA,U      A0,' '            ASSUME ANOTHER SPACE  CV
)@@G@@@G@@@@          TZ        R2                BUT WAS SKIP FLAG PREVIOUSLYCW
)@@G@@ SET? @F@@@@          LA,U      A0,'*'            YES, INDICATE SKIPPED CX
)@@G@@LINES @F@@@@          E$CHAR    .                 EDIT A SPACE OR ASTERICY
)@@G@@SK    @F@@@@          LR        R2,WPL            GET # OF WORDS PER LINCZ
)@@G@@E     @D@@@@          JGD       R2,$+1            LESS 1 FOR JGD  @[@@@@DA
)@@G@@.     @H@@@@. EDIT PROPER NUMBER OF WORDS PER LINE.  THE LAST LINE MAY BDB
)@@G@@E A PARTIAL LINE. @[@@@@.     @G@@@@WORDLOOP  E$OCTF    12,0,*X4        DC
)@@G@@  EDIT VALUE AND POINT TO NEXT WORD @E@@@@          E$SKIP    2         DD
)@@G@@        2 SPACES BETWEEN WORDS@E@@@@          LA,U      A0,0,X4         DE
)@@G@@  GET CURRENT WORD INDEX@E@@@@          ANA       A0,BUFAD          MAKEDF
)@@G@@ IT RELATIVE TO 0 @D@@@@          TLE       A0,NWRDS          ALL DONE YDG
)@@G@@ET?   @F@@@@.                                     IF SO, MAY BE PARTIAL DH
)@@G@@LINE  @G@@@@          JGD       R2,WORDLOOP       NO, GO BACK AND FINISHDI
)@@G@@ THIS LINE  @G@@@@          P$RINT    POUT              DONE WITH THIS LDJ
)@@G@@INE:  PRINT IT    @[@@@@.     @H@@@@. SAVE LAST WORD OF THIS LINE FOR SKDK
)@@G@@IP COMPARISON, AND SET FOR NEXT LINE.     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@NEXTLINE  LADL
)@@G@@,U      A0,0,X4           GET CURRENT WORD INDEX@F@@@@          ANA,U   DM
)@@G@@  A0,1              BACK UP TO LAST WORD PRINTED@G@@@@          LA      DN
)@@G@@  A0,0,A0           PICK UP THE LAST WORD PRINTED     @F@@@@          SADO
)@@G@@        A0,LASTWD         AND STORE IT FOR SKIP TEST  @E@@@@          JGDP
)@@G@@D       R4,LINELOOP       MORE LINES?  DO THEM  @F@@@@          J       DQ
)@@G@@  0,X10             ALL DONE:  RETURN TO CALLER @ @@@@          OFF     DR
)@@G@@  SNAPSUB   @ @@@@          OFF       SNAPOK    @#@@@@          END     DS
)@@G@@___T TO A1  @G@@@@      *[S@@@*SDFF*@A@@@@. @MFD INITIALIZATION - PHASE DT
)@@G@@1     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. ALL USE OF INFOR$ MUST BE COMPLETE BY THE END DU
)@@G@@OF THIS ROUTINE, SINCE  @G@@@@. INFOR$ IS COLLECTED IN THE INIT1 SEGMENTDV
)@@G@@, WHICH GETS OVERLAID AFTER   @#@@@@. INITIALIZATION. @[@@@@.     @^@@@@DW
)@@G@@          AXR$      .   @F@@@@          CONFIG    .                 DEFIDX
)@@G@@NE CONFIG PARAMETERS    @D@@@@          EQUFS     .                 DEFIDY
)@@G@@NE EQUF'S   @[@@@@.     @G@@@@PNAME     'MFD         '              ASSUDZ
)@@G@@MED PROCESSOR NAME (12 CHAR)  @D@@@@. REMOTE LOAD TABLE FOR C/Y OPTION SEA
)@@G@@PEC MASK, ETC.    @[@@@@.     @ @@@@ACLD      LA,S1     A0,0,X2   @ @@@@EB
